form\n\n10. **Check Status** - Application moves to \\\"submitted\\\" state\n\n## 🤖 AI Gateway\n\nThe system includes a provider-agnostic AI gateway supporting:\n\n- **Mock Provider** (default) - No API costs, deterministic responses\n- **Anthropic** - Claude 3.5 Sonnet / Haiku\n- **OpenAI** - GPT-4 / GPT-3.5 Turbo\n\n### Configuration\n\n```bash\n# Use mock (no API key needed)\nexport AI_PROVIDER=mock\n\n# Use Anthropic\nexport AI_PROVIDER=anthropic\nexport ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=sk-ant-...\n\n# Use OpenAI\nexport AI_PROVIDER=openai\nexport OPENAI_API_KEY=sk-...\n```\n\n### Structured Outputs\n\nAll AI responses use validated Pydantic schemas:\n- `ExtractedJob` - Job data extraction\n- `JobClassification` - Category assignment\n- `MatchScore` - Transparent scoring with dimension breakdown\n- `ResumeSelection` - Resume selection with rationale\n- `ResumeTailoring` - Resume modifications with provenance\n- `ReviewResult` - Application review findings\n\n## 🗄️ Database Schema\n\n### Core Tables\n\n- **users** - Authentication\n- **profiles** - User profile with work preferences\n- **resume_families** - Resume categories (e.g., \\\"Data Engineering\\\")\n- **resume_versions** - Versioned resume files with parsed data\n- **canonical_jobs** - Normalized job postings\n- **applications** - Application records with state\n- **workflow_tasks** - Background job tracking\n- **audit_events** - Complete audit trail\n- **model_calls** - AI usage and cost tracking\n\nAll tables use:\n- UUID primary keys\n- `created_at`, `updated_at` timestamps\n- Foreign key constraints\n- Status indexes\n\n## 🔒 Security & Privacy\n\n### Authentication\n- JWT tokens with bcrypt password hashing\n- 24-hour token expiration\n- Secure HTTP-only cookies (production)\n\n### Data Protection\n- Sensitive fields separated from general profile\n- Field-level minimization (agents only see needed data)\n- Redaction in logs and AI calls\n- No secrets in version control\n\n### Browser Automation\n- Respects CAPTCHA and auth controls\n- Pauses workflow when anti-bot controls detected\n- Screenshots stored locally, retention configurable\n- No circumvention of site restrictions\n\n## 🎨 Frontend Features\n\n### Dashboard\n- Jobs discovered today\n- Applications pending review\n- Match score distribution\n- Recent activity feed\n\n### Profile Management\n- Personal information\n- Work history with date validation\n- Education records\n- Skills with proficiency levels\n- Projects and accomplishments\n\n### Resume Center\n- Multiple resume families\n- Upload and parsing\n- Version history\n- Approval workflow\n- Diff viewer for tailored variants\n\n### Job Inbox\n- Table and card views\n- Match score badges\n- Filters: category, score, location, status\n- Click to view detailed match analysis\n\n### Application Tracker\n- Kanban board (Preparing → Review → Ready → Applied)\n- Application detail with resume diff\n- Answer review with risk classification\n- Approve/edit controls\n\n## 🔄 State Machines\n\n### Job Status\ndiscovered → extracting → scored → saved → shortlisted → preparing → ready_for_review → approved\n\n### Application Pipeline\nnot_started → draft → awaiting_review → approved → browser_running → submitted → confirmed\n\n### Workflow Status\npending → running → waiting_user_input → completed / failed / cancelled\n\nAll transitions are validated and logged.\n\n## 🧩 Extending the System\n\n### Adding a New ATS Adapter\n\n1. Create `/apps/browser-worker/browser_worker/adapters/newats_adapter.py`\n2. Extend `ATSAdapter` base class\n3. Implement methods: `detect()`, `inspect_form()`, `fill_field()`, etc.\n4. Register in adapter registry\n5. Add tests in `tests/test_adapters.py`\n\n### Adding a New AI Agent\n\n1. Create `/backend/app/agents/new_agent.py`\n2. Extend `BaseAgent` class\n3. Define Pydantic response schema\n4. Implement `execute()` method with prompt\n5. Add to agent registry\n6. Create evaluation dataset in `tests/evaluations/`\n\n### Adding an AI Provider\n\n1. Create `/backend/app/ai_gateway/providers/newprovider_provider.py`\n2. Extend `AIProvider` base class\n3. Implement `generate()` and `generate_json()` methods\n4. Add provider configuration\n5. Update provider factory\n\n## 📊 Monitoring & Observability\n\n### Logs\n- Structured JSON logs (development: pretty-printed)\n- Request IDs for tracing\n- Sensitive data redacted\n\n### Metrics (Future)\n- Jobs ingested per day\n- Match score distribution\n- Application success rate\n- Browser automation success rate\n- AI cost per application\n\n### Audit Trail\n- All API calls logged\n- All AI decisions with explanations\n- All browser actions with screenshots\n- State transitions with timestamps\n\n## 🚧 Current Limitations (Phase 1)\n\n- Single-user system (multi-tenant support planned)\n- Mock AI provider only (real LLM integration ready but requires API keys)\n- One mock ATS adapter (Greenhouse, Lever, Ashby planned)\n- Database-backed workflows (Temporal migration planned)\n- Manual job import only (scheduled discovery planned)\n- No email integration yet\n- No analytics dashboard yet\n- Basic authentication (OAuth2 planned)\n\n## 📈 Roadmap\n\n### Phase 2: Matching & Resume Selection\n- Advanced hybrid matching (rules + semantic + LLM)\n- Resume selection agent with performance tracking\n- Match explanation with evidence matrix\n\n### Phase 3: Tailoring & Review\n- Resume tailoring with provenance\n- Claim validation against profile facts\n- Independent review agent\n- Resume diff viewer\n\n### Phase 4: Browser-Assisted Applications\n- Greenhouse adapter\n- Lever adapter\n- Ashby adapter\n- Manual takeover support\n- Video recording\n\n### Phase 5: ATS Adapters\n- Workday adapter\n- SmartRecruiters adapter\n- Generic adapter improvements\n\n### Phase 6: Discovery Automation\n- Scheduled search profiles\n- Company watchlists\n- Public ATS ingestion\n- Browser extension\n\n### Phase 7: Tracking & Analytics\n- Email integration\n- Interview scheduling\n- Follow-up reminders\n- Outcome tracking\n- Search strategy recommendations\n\n### Phase 8: Controlled Autopilot\n- Trusted domain rules\n- Quality thresholds\n- Daily limits\n- Independent review requirement\n- Kill switch\n\n## 🤝 Contributing\n\nThis is a personal project optimized for a single job seeker. Enterprise features (multi-tenant, advanced analytics, etc.) are deferred until the core workflow is solid.\n\n## 📝 License\n\nPrivate project. All rights reserved.\n\n## 🆘 Troubleshooting\n\n### Services won't start\n```bash\n# Check Docker\ndocker ps\ndocker-compose logs\n\n# Rebuild containers\ndocker-compose down\ndocker-compose build\ndocker-compose up -d\n```\n\n### Database connection errors\n```bash\n# Check PostgreSQL\nmake shell-db\n\n# Reset database\nmake clean\nmake start\nmake migrate\n```\n\n### Frontend can't connect to API\n- Check `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL` in `apps/web/.env.local`\n- Verify API is running: `curl http://localhost:8000/health`\n- Check CORS settings in `backend/main.py`\n\n### Browser worker fails\n- Check Playwright installation: `playwright install chromium`\n- Verify mock ATS is running: `curl http://localhost:8080`\n- Check screenshots directory exists and is writable\n\n## 📞 Support\n\nFor issues or questions:\n1. │\n│  │  └──────────┴──────────┴──────────┴──────────────────┘  │ │\n│  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │\n│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │\n│  │  Services: FormInspector, FieldMapper, CheckpointMgr   │ │\n│  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │\n└─────────────────────────┬─────────────────────────────────────┘\n                          │ HTTP\n┌─────────────────────────▼─────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                    Target ATS Sites                            │\n│     Mock ATS  |  Greenhouse  |  Lever  |  Ashby  |  Others    │\n└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n\n┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                    File Storage (MinIO)                        │\n│  • Resume PDFs     • Screenshots     • Documents              │\n└───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## Data Flow: Complete Vertical Slice\n\n### 1. User Registration & Profile Creation\n```\nUser → Frontend → POST /api/auth/register → Backend\n                                          → Hash password\n                                          → Create user record\n                                          → Return JWT token\n\nUser → Frontend → POST /api/profile → Backend\n                                    → Create profile\n                                    → Store work history, skills\n```\n\n### 2. Resume Upload\n```\nUser → Frontend → POST /api/resumes → Backend\n                                    → Upload file to MinIO\n                                    → Calculate hash\n                                    → Parse PDF (mock parser)\n                                    → Extract structured data\n                                    → Create ResumeFamily + ResumeVersion\n                                    → Status: needs_review\n```\n\n### 3. Job Import\n```\nUser → Frontend → POST /api/jobs/import-url → Backend\n                                            → Fetch URL\n                                            → Create WorkflowTask\n                                            → Queue for processing\n\nBackground Worker:\n  → ExtractionAgent.extract(raw_html)\n     → AI Gateway (Mock Provider)\n     → Return ExtractedJob schema\n  → ClassificationAgent.classify(job_data)\n     → Return JobClassification\n  → Save CanonicalJob\n  → Status: scored\n\n  → MatchingAgent.score(job, profile)\n     → Calculate dimension scores\n     → Return MatchScore with explanation\n  → Update job.score\n```\n\n### 4. Application Preparation\n```\nUser → Frontend → POST /api/applications → Backend\n                                         → Create Application record\n                                         → Create WorkflowTask\n\nBackground Worker:\n  → ResumeSelectionAgent.select(job, resumes, profile)\n     → Return selected_resume_id + rationale\n  \n  → TailoringAgent.tailor(job, resume, profile)\n     → Generate requirement-evidence matrix\n     → Reorder/rewrite bullets (preserve facts)\n     → Return ResumeTailoring with provenance\n  \n  → QuestionAgent.answer(questions, profile)\n     → Classify risk level\n     → Generate answers from verified facts\n     → Return answers with sources\n  \n  → ReviewAgent.review(application, resume, answers)\n     → Independent verification\n     → Check for contradictions\n     → Check claim provenance\n     → Return ReviewResult\n  \n  → Update Application status: awaiting_review\n```\n\n### 5. User Review & Approval\n```\nUser → Frontend → GET /api/applications/{id}\n                → Display:\n                   • Resume diff viewer\n                   • Generated answers\n                   • Risk classifications\n                   • Review findings\n                \nUser approves → POST /api/applications/{id}/approve\n             → Update status: approved\n```\n\n### 6. Browser Submission\n```\nUser → Frontend → POST /api/applications/{id}/start-browser\n\nBackend → Create WorkflowTask\n       → Queue for browser-worker\n\nBrowser Worker:\n  1. process_application(application_id)\n  2. Get application data from API\n  3. Launch Playwright browser\n  4. Navigate to job URL\n  5. Detect ATS type (check data-ats attribute)\n  6. Select adapter (MockATSAdapter)\n  7. inspect_form()\n     → Extract all fields with labels\n     → Detect required fields\n     → Map to canonical names\n  8. For each field:\n     → Get answer from application data\n     → fill_field(field, answer)\n  9. upload_document(resume_file)\n  10. Create checkpoint\n  11. Pause (Assisted Mode)\n      → Status: paused\n      → Waiting for user confirmation\n\nUser reviews preview → POST /api/applications/{id}/resume\n                    → Continue workflow\n\nBrowser Worker:\n  12. Resume from checkpoint\n  13. preview_submission()\n  14. submit()\n  15. detect_confirmation()\n      → Look for success indicators\n      → Extract application ID\n  16. Take final screenshot\n  17. Update Application status: confirmed\n  18. Create AuditEvent\n```\n\n## State Transitions\n\n### Job States\n```\ndiscovered\n  ↓ (extraction starts)\nextracting\n  ↓ (data extracted, classified)\nscored\n  ↓ (user views)\nsaved / shortlisted\n  ↓ (user decides to apply)\npreparing\n  ↓ (application generated)\nready_for_review\n  ↓ (user approves)\napproved\n```\n\n### Application Pipeline States\n```\nnot_started\n  ↓\ndraft\n  ↓ (generation complete)\nawaiting_review\n  ↓ (user approves)\napproved\n  ↓ (browser starts)\nbrowser_running\n  ↓ (pause point)\npaused\n  ↓ (user confirms)\nbrowser_running\n  ↓ (submission complete)\nsubmitted\n  ↓ (confirmation detected)\nconfirmed\n```\n\n### Workflow States\n```\npending → running → completed\n             ↓\n       waiting_user_input\n             ↓ (user responds)\n          running → completed\n\nOR\n\npending → running → failed\n                     ↓ (retryable)\n                  pending (retry)\n```\n\n## Security Model\n\n### Authentication Flow\n1. User submits credentials\n2. Backend validates with bcrypt\n3. Generate JWT with user_id claim\n4. Return token (expires in 24h)\n5. Frontend stores in HTTP-only cookie\n6. All API calls include Authorization header\n7. Backend validates token on each request\n8. Dependency injection provides current_user\n\n### Authorization Rules\n- Users can only access their own data\n- All API routes check user_id from JWT\n- Database queries filter by user_id\n- File URLs are pre-signed (expire in 1 hour)\n\n### Sensitive Data Handling\n- Passwords hashed with bcrypt\n- JWT secrets in environment variables\n- Sensitive profile fields in separate table (future)\n- AI calls redact SSN, passwords, etc.\n- Browser screenshots redact sensitive fields\n- Audit logs exclude full sensitive values\n\n### Browser Security\n- No CAPTCHA circumvention\n- Pause on authentication required\n- Restricted to approved domains\n- No arbitrary code execution\n- Screenshot retention configurable\n- User can disable automation per site\n\n## Scaling Strategy (Future)\n\n### Phase 1 (Current)\n- Single server\n- Docker Compose\n- Database-backed workflows\n- Single background worker\n\n### Phase 2\n- Multiple API instances behind load balancer\n- Separate worker pool\n- Redis for distributed locks\n- Shared MinIO instance\n\n### Phase 3\n- Temporal for workflow orchestration\n- Separate browser worker pool\n- Queue-based job distribution\n- Horizontal scaling\n\n### Phase 4\n- Multi-region deployment\n- Read replicas for database\n- CDN for static assets\n- Elasticsearch for search\n- Message queue (RabbitMQ/Kafka)\n\n## Technology Stack Justification\n\n**FastAPI**: \n- Modern async Python framework\n- Automatic OpenAPI docs\n- Pydantic validation built-in\n- High performance\n\n**Next.js 14**:\n- App Router with server components\n- Built-in API routes\n- TypeScript support\n- Excellent developer experience\n\n**PostgreSQL**:\n- ACID compliance\n- JSON support (JSONB)\n- Full-text search\n- pgvector for embeddings (future)\n- Mature and reliable\n\n**Playwright**:\n- Cross-browser support\n- Async API\n- Built-in screenshots\n- Network interception\n- Better than Selenium for modern sites\n\n**Docker Compose**:\n- Local development parity with production\n- Service isolation\n- Easy dependency management\n- One-command startup\n\n**MinIO**:\n- S3-compatible API\n- Self-hosted\n- No cloud vendor lock-in\n- Easy migration to AWS S3\n\n## Monitoring & Observability (Future)\n\n- Structured JSON logs → Elasticsearch → Kibana\n- Metrics → Prometheus → Grafana\n- Traces → Jaeger/Zipkin\n- Errors → Sentry\n- Uptime → UptimeRobot\n\n## Deployment Options\n\n### Development (Current)\n```bash\ndocker-compose up\n```\n\n### Production - Docker Compose\n```bash\ndocker-compose -f docker-compose.prod.yml up -d\n```\n\n### Production - Kubernetes (Future)\n```\n- Deployment per service\n- StatefulSet for PostgreSQL\n- PersistentVolumes for data\n- Ingress for routing\n- HorizontalPodAutoscaler\n```\n\nEOF\necho \"ARCHITECTURE.md created\"'"

## 🎯 Vertical Slice Flow

The complete end-to-end workflow works:

1. **Register** → Create account with email/password
2. **Profile** → Enter work history, skills, preferences
3. **Resume** → Upload PDF, parse, approve as base
4. **Job Import** → Paste URL, extract structured data
5. **Match Score** → Transparent scoring with dimensions
6. **Prepare** → AI tailors resume, generates answers
7. **Review** → Independent review agent checks claims
8. **Approve** → User reviews diff and approves
9. **Submit** → Browser fills form, pauses for confirmation
10. **Track** → Status updated, audit log recorded

## 🔄 State Machines

**JobStatus**: discovered → extracting → scored → approved  
**ApplicationPipeline**: draft → awaiting_review → approved → submitted → confirmed  
**WorkflowStatus**: pending → running → completed/failed

## 🚧 Known Limitations (By Design)

- Single-user system (multi-tenant planned for later)
- Mock AI only by default (real LLMs require API keys)
- One ATS adapter (Greenhouse/Lever/Ashby interfaces ready)
- Manual job import (scheduled discovery planned)
- No email integration yet (Phase 7)
- Basic authentication (OAuth2 planned)

## 🛠️ Technology Stack

- **Backend**: Python 3.11, FastAPI, SQLAlchemy, Alembic, Pydantic
- **Frontend**: Next.js 14, TypeScript, React, Tailwind CSS, shadcn/ui
- **Database**: PostgreSQL 15 with JSONB support
- **Cache**: Redis 7
- **Storage**: MinIO (S3-compatible)
- **Automation**: Playwright with Chromium
- **Container**: Docker Compose

### Future Phases:
- **Phase 2**: Advanced matching with semantic search

## 💡 Key Design Decisions

1. **Database-backed workflows** instead of Temporal (Phase 1 simplicity, migration path preserved)
2. **Mock AI provider** as default (zero cost testing)
3. **Assisted mode** default (human approval before submission)
4. **Explicit state machines** (no implicit state transitions)
5. **Provenance tracking** (all AI claims trace to verified facts)
6. **Idempotent operations** (safe to retry)
7. **Container-first** (all services in Docker)

Create SearchProfile Model\nFile: `backend/app/models/search_profile.py`\n```python\nclass SearchProfile(Base):\n    __tablename__ = \"search_profiles\"\n    id = Column(UUID(as_uuid=True), primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4)\n    user_id = Column(UUID(as_uuid=True), ForeignKey(\"users.id\"))\n    name = Column(String, nullable=False)\n    enabled = Column(Boolean, default=True)\n    career_categories = Column(ARRAY(String))  # e.g. [\"data_engineering\", \"software_engineering\"]\n    include_titles = Column(ARRAY(String))\n    exclude_titles = Column(ARRAY(String))\n    include_skills = Column(ARRAY(String))\n    exclude_skills = Column(ARRAY(String))\n    locations = Column(ARRAY(String))\n    remote_policy = Column(String)  # \"remote\", \"hybrid\", \"onsite\", \"any\"\n    min_salary = Column(Integer)\n    employment_types = Column(ARRAY(String))\n    seniority_levels = Column(ARRAY(String))\n    companies = Column(ARRAY(String))\n    excluded_companies = Column(ARRAY(String))\n    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)\n    updated_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, onupdate=datetime.utcnow)\n```\n\n### 2. Add JobMatchScore Model\nFile: `backend/app/models/job_match.py`\n```python\nclass JobMatchScore(Base):\n    __tablename__ = \"job_match_scores\"\n    id = Column(UUID(as_uuid=True), primary_key=True, default=uuid.uuid4)\n    job_id = Column(UUID(as_uuid=True), ForeignKey(\"canonical_jobs.id\"))\n    user_id = Column(UUID(as_uuid=True), ForeignKey(\"users.id\"))\n    overall_score = Column(Integer)  # 0-100\n    skill_score = Column(Float)\n    experience_score = Column(Float)\n    seniority_score = Column(Float)\n    location_score = Column(Float)\n    salary_score = Column(Float)\n    hard_blockers = Column(JSON)\n    strong_matches = Column(JSON)\n    soft_gaps = Column(JSON)\n    missing_info = Column(JSON)\n    recommended_action = Column(String)  # reject, save_for_later, prepare_application, etc.\n    explanation = Column(Text)\n    matched_resume_id = Column(UUID(as_uuid=True), ForeignKey(\"resume_versions.id\"), nullable=True)\n    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)\n```\n\n### 3. Create Migration\n```bash\ncd backend\nalembic revision -m \"add_search_profiles_and_matching\"\n# Add both tables to migration\n```\n\n### 4. Implement Matching Agent\nFile: `backend/app/agents/matching_agent.py`\n```python\nclass MatchingAgent(BaseAgent):\n    async def score_job(self, job: CanonicalJob, profile: Profile, resumes: List[ResumeVersion]) -> MatchScore:\n        # Deterministic scoring\n        skill_score = self._calculate_skill_match(job, profile)\n        experience_score = self._calculate_experience_match(job, profile)\n        seniority_score = self._calculate_seniority_match(job, profile)\n        location_score = self._calculate_location_match(job, profile)\n        salary_score = self._calculate_salary_match(job, profile)\n        \n        # Check hard blockers\n        hard_blockers = self._check_hard_blockers(job, profile)\n        \n        # Calculate overall score (weighted average)\n        overall = (skill_score * 0.35 + experience_score * 0.25 + \n                   seniority_score * 0.15 + location_score * 0.15 + \n                   salary_score * 0.10)\n        \n        # Use AI for explanation\n        explanation = await self._generate_explanation(job, profile, overall, skill_score, ...)\n        \n        # Determine action\n        action = self._recommend_action(overall, hard_blockers)\n        \n        return MatchScore(...)\n```\n\n### 5. Implement Resume Selection Agent\nFile: `backend/app/agents/resume_selection_agent.py`\n```python\nclass ResumeSelectionAgent(BaseAgent):\n    async def select_resume(self, job: CanonicalJob, resumes: List[ResumeVersion], profile: Profile) -> ResumeSelectionResult:\n        # Score each resume against job requirements\n        scores = []\n        for resume in resumes:\n            coverage = self._calculate_coverage(resume, job)\n            relevance = self._calculate_relevance(resume, job)\n            recency = self._calculate_recency(resume)\n            performance = resume.usage_stats.get(\"interview_rate\", 0)\n            \n            total_score = coverage * 0.4 + relevance * 0.3 + recency * 0.2 + performance * 0.1\n            scores.append((resume, total_score))\n        \n        # Select best\n        best_resume, best_score = max(scores, key=lambda x: x[1])\n        \n        # Generate rationale with AI\n        rationale = await self._explain_selection(best_resume, job, scores)\n        \n        return ResumeSelectionResult(\n            selected_resume_id=best_resume.id,\n            selection_rationale=rationale,\n            alternatives=[...],\n            missing_coverage=[...],\n            tailoring_recommended=best_score < 0.8\n        )\n```\n\n### 6. Create API Routes\nFile: `backend/app/api/routes/search_profiles.py`\n```python\n@router.post(\"/\", response_model=SearchProfileResponse)\nasync def create_search_profile(...)\n\n@router.get(\"/\", response_model=List[SearchProfileResponse])\nasync def list_search_profiles(...)\n\n@router.patch(\"/{id}\", response_model=SearchProfileResponse)\nasync def update_search_profile(...)\n\n@router.delete(\"/{id}\")\nasync def delete_search_profile(...)\n```\n\nFile: `backend/app/api/routes/jobs.py` - Add endpoints:\n```python\n@router.post(\"/{job_id}/match\", response_model=JobMatchScoreResponse)\nasync def calculate_match_score(job_id: UUID, current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user)):\n    # Run matching agent\n    # Save JobMatchScore\n    # Return score with explanation\n\n@router.get(\"/{job_id}/match\", response_model=JobMatchScoreResponse)\nasync def get_match_score(job_id: UUID, current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user)):\n    # Return existing match score\n\n@router.post(\"/{job_id}/select-resume\", response_model=ResumeSelectionResponse)\nasync def select_best_resume(job_id: UUID, current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user)):\n    # Run resume selection agent\n    # Return selected resume with rationale\n```\n\n### 7. Add Schemas\nCreate Pydantic schemas for:\n- SearchProfile (CRUD)\n- JobMatchScore (response)\n- ResumeSelectionResult (response)\n\n### 8. Create Tests\nFile: `backend/tests/test_matching.py`\n- Test skill matching calculation\n- Test hard blocker detection\n- Test overall score calculation\n- Test recommended action logic\n\nFile: `backend/tests/test_resume_selection.py`\n- Test resume coverage calculation\n- Test resume selection logic\n- Test rationale generation\n\n### 9. Seed Test Data\nCreate sample search profiles and resumes for testing.\n\n## Execution Steps\n\n1. Create models and migration\n2. Run migration\n3. Implement agents (use mock AI provider)\n4. - **Location matching**: Remote/hybrid/onsite preference scoring
- **Salary matching**: Compensation expectation evaluation

- **Coverage calculation**: Skill match percentage (Jaccard similarity)

- **Recency scoring**: Age-based scoring (recent = better)
- **Performance scoring**: Historical interview rate tracking
- **Multi-factor selection**: 40% coverage, 30% relevance, 20% recency, 10% performance
- **Gap analysis**: Identifies missing skills for tailoring
- **Alternative suggestions**: Ranks top alternatives
